\DoxyCodeLine{85 EIGEN\_STRONG\_INLINE Packet4f shuffle1(\textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet4f\& m, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} mask)\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{86   \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* a = \textcolor{keyword}{reinterpret\_cast<}\textcolor{keyword}{const }\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}*\textcolor{keyword}{>}(\&m);}
\DoxyCodeLine{87   Packet4f res = \{*(a + (mask \& 3)), *(a + ((mask >> 2) \& 3)), *(a + ((mask >> 4) \& 3 )), *(a + ((mask >> 6) \& 3))\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{88   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} res;}
\DoxyCodeLine{89 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{90 }
\DoxyCodeLine{91 \textcolor{comment}{// fuctionally equivalent to \_mm\_shuffle\_ps in SSE when interleave}}
\DoxyCodeLine{92 \textcolor{comment}{// == false (i.e. shuffle<false>(m, n, mask) equals \_mm\_shuffle\_ps(m, n, mask)),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{93 \textcolor{comment}{// interleave m and n when interleave == true. Currently used in LU/arch/InverseSize4.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{94 \textcolor{comment}{// to enable a shared implementation for fast inversion of matrices of size 4. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{95 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}erleave> }
\DoxyCodeLine{96 EIGEN\_STRONG\_INLINE Packet4f shuffle2(\textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet4f \&m, \textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet4f \&n, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} mask)}
\DoxyCodeLine{97 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{98   \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* a = \textcolor{keyword}{reinterpret\_cast<}\textcolor{keyword}{const }\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}*\textcolor{keyword}{>}(\&m);}
\DoxyCodeLine{99   \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* b = \textcolor{keyword}{reinterpret\_cast<}\textcolor{keyword}{const }\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}*\textcolor{keyword}{>}(\&n);}
\DoxyCodeLine{100   Packet4f res = \{*(a + (mask \& 3)), *(a + ((mask >> 2) \& 3)), *(b + ((mask >> 4) \& 3)), *(b + ((mask >> 6) \& 3))\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{101   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} res;}
\DoxyCodeLine{102 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{152   \textcolor{comment}{// \_\_builtin\_prefetch tends to do nothing on ARM64 compilers because the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{153   \textcolor{comment}{// prefetch instructions there are too detailed for \_\_builtin\_prefetch to map}}
\DoxyCodeLine{154   \textcolor{comment}{// meaningfully to them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{155 \textcolor{preprocessor}{  \#define EIGEN\_ARM\_PREFETCH(ADDR)  \_\_asm\_\_ \_\_volatile\_\_("{}prfm pldl1keep, [\%[addr]]\(\backslash\)n"{}} ::[addr] "{}r"{}(ADDR) : );}
\DoxyCodeLine{156 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif EIGEN\_HAS\_BUILTIN(\_\_builtin\_prefetch) || EIGEN\_COMP\_GNUC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{157 \textcolor{preprocessor}{  \#define EIGEN\_ARM\_PREFETCH(ADDR) \_\_builtin\_prefetch(ADDR);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{158 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif defined \_\_pld}}

\DoxyCodeLine{160 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif EIGEN\_ARCH\_ARM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{161 \textcolor{preprocessor}{  \#define EIGEN\_ARM\_PREFETCH(ADDR) \_\_asm\_\_ \_\_volatile\_\_ ("{}pld [\%[addr]]\(\backslash\)n"{}} :: [addr] "{}r"{} (ADDR) : );}
\DoxyCodeLine{162 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}

\DoxyCodeLine{954 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<> EIGEN\_STRONG\_INLINE Packet2f pdiv<Packet2f>(\textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet2f\& a, \textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet2f\& b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{955 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{956 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if EIGEN\_ARCH\_ARM64}}
\DoxyCodeLine{957   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} vdiv\_f32(a,b);}
\DoxyCodeLine{958 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{959   Packet2f inv, restep, div;}
\DoxyCodeLine{960 }
\DoxyCodeLine{961   \textcolor{comment}{// NEON does not offer a divide instruction, we have to do a reciprocal approximation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{962   \textcolor{comment}{// However NEON in contrast to other SIMD engines (AltiVec/SSE), offers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{963   \textcolor{comment}{// a reciprocal estimate AND a reciprocal step -\/which saves a few instructions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{964   \textcolor{comment}{// vrecpeq\_f32() returns an estimate to 1/b, which we will finetune with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{965   \textcolor{comment}{// Newton-\/Raphson and vrecpsq\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{966   inv = vrecpe\_f32(b);}
\DoxyCodeLine{967 }
\DoxyCodeLine{968   \textcolor{comment}{// This returns a differential, by which we will have to multiply inv to get a better}}
\DoxyCodeLine{969   \textcolor{comment}{// approximation of 1/b.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{970   restep = vrecps\_f32(b, inv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{971   inv = vmul\_f32(restep, inv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{972 }
\DoxyCodeLine{973   \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, multiply a by 1/b and get the wanted result of the division.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{974   div = vmul\_f32(a, inv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{975 }
\DoxyCodeLine{976   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} div;}
\DoxyCodeLine{977 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{978 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{979 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<> EIGEN\_STRONG\_INLINE Packet4f pdiv<Packet4f>(\textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet4f\& a, \textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet4f\& b)}

\DoxyCodeLine{988   \textcolor{comment}{// a reciprocal estimate AND a reciprocal step -\/which saves a few instructions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{989   \textcolor{comment}{// vrecpeq\_f32() returns an estimate to 1/b, which we will finetune with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{990   \textcolor{comment}{// Newton-\/Raphson and vrecpsq\_f32()}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2984 EIGEN\_ALWAYS\_INLINE \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} ptranspose\_impl(PacketBlock<Packet, 16>\& kernel) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2985   EIGEN\_UNROLL\_LOOP}
\DoxyCodeLine{2986   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i=0; i<4; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2987     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = (1 << i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2988     EIGEN\_UNROLL\_LOOP}
\DoxyCodeLine{2989     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} j=0; j<m; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2990       \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = (1 << (3-\/i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2991       EIGEN\_UNROLL\_LOOP}
\DoxyCodeLine{2992       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} k=0; k<n; ++k) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2993         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} idx = 2*j*n+k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2994         zip\_in\_place(kernel.packet[idx], kernel.packet[idx + n]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2995       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2996     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3266 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<> EIGEN\_STRONG\_INLINE Packet4uc psqrt(\textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet4uc\& a) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3267   uint8x8\_t x = vreinterpret\_u8\_u32(vdup\_n\_u32(a));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3268   uint8x8\_t res = vdup\_n\_u8(0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3269   uint8x8\_t add = vdup\_n\_u8(0x8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3270   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < 4; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3271   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3272     \textcolor{keyword}{const} uint8x8\_t temp = vorr\_u8(res, add);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3274     add = vshr\_n\_u8(add, 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} vget\_lane\_u32(vreinterpret\_u32\_u8(res), 0);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3462 EIGEN\_STRONG\_INLINE Packet4bf F32ToBf16(\textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet4f\& p)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3463 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3464   \textcolor{comment}{// See the scalar implementation in BFloat16.h for a comprehensible explanation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3465   \textcolor{comment}{// of this fast rounding algorithm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3466   Packet4ui input = \textcolor{keyword}{reinterpret\_cast<}Packet4ui\textcolor{keyword}{>}(p);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3468   \textcolor{comment}{// lsb = (input >> 16) \& 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3469   Packet4ui lsb =  vandq\_u32(vshrq\_n\_u32(input, 16), vdupq\_n\_u32(1));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3471   \textcolor{comment}{// rounding\_bias = 0x7fff + lsb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3472   Packet4ui rounding\_bias = vaddq\_u32(lsb, vdupq\_n\_u32(0x7fff));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3474   \textcolor{comment}{// input += rounding\_bias}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475   input = vaddq\_u32(input, rounding\_bias);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3477   \textcolor{comment}{// input = input >> 16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478   input = vshrq\_n\_u32(input, 16);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3480   \textcolor{comment}{// Replace float-\/nans by bfloat16-\/nans, that is 0x7fc0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481   \textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet4ui bf16\_nan = vdupq\_n\_u32(0x7fc0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482   \textcolor{keyword}{const} Packet4ui mask = vceqq\_f32(p, p);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483   input = vbslq\_u32(mask, input, bf16\_nan);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3485   \textcolor{comment}{// output = static\_cast<uint16\_t>(input)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3486   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} vmovn\_u32(input);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3487 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3703 \textcolor{comment}{// Clang 3.5 in the iOS toolchain has an ICE triggered by NEON intrisics for double.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3704 \textcolor{comment}{// Confirmed at least with \_\_apple\_build\_version\_\_ = 6000054.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3705 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef \_\_apple\_build\_version\_\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3706 \textcolor{comment}{// Let's hope that by the time \_\_apple\_build\_version\_\_ hits the 601* range, the bug will be fixed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3707 \textcolor{comment}{// https://gist.github.com/yamaya/2924292 suggests that the 3 first digits are only updated with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3708 \textcolor{comment}{// major toolchain updates.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3709 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define EIGEN\_APPLE\_DOUBLE\_NEON\_BUG (\_\_apple\_build\_version\_\_ < 6010000)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3710 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
